/**
 * @returns string category or product code by URL
 */
const getCategory = () => {
  var splitedURL = window.location.href.split("/");

  if (getPageType() == "PLP") {
    if (splitedURL.indexOf("category") != -1) {
      return splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("category") + 1].trim();
    } else if (splitedURL.indexOf("collection") != -1) {
      return (
        splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("collection") + 1].trim().split("?")[0] ||
        "none"
      );
    }
    return null;
  } else if (getPageType() == "PDP") {
    if (splitedURL.indexOf("product") != -1) {
      return splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("product") + 1].trim();
    }
  } else if (getPageType() == "SLP") {
    return "S";
  } else if (getPageType() == "Page") {
    if (splitedURL.indexOf("page") != -1) {
      return (
        splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("page") + 1].trim().split("?")[0] ||
        "none"
      );
    }
  }
  return "none";
};

/**
 *
 * @param parameterName string name of parameter to search
 * @returns parameter value if found or else null
 */
const getParameter = (parameterName) => {
  var params = window.location.search;
  params = params.replace("?", "").split("&");

  params = params.filter(function (p) {
    return p.includes(parameterName + "=");
  });

  return params.length > 0 ? params[0].split("=")[1] : null;
};

/**
 *
 * @returns string page type by URL
 */
const getPageType = () => {
  if (
    /category/i.test(window.location.href) ||
    /collection/i.test(window.location.href)
  ) {
    return "PLP";
  }

  if (/search/i.test(window.location.href)) {
    return "SLP";
  }

  if (/product/i.test(window.location.href)) {
    return "PDP";
  }

  if (/page/i.test(window.location.href)) {
    return "Page";
  }

  return "Home";
};

const createDigitalData = () => {
  if (typeof window.digitalData === "undefined") {
    window.digitalData = {};
  }

  if (window.digitalData) {
    if (typeof window.digitalData.storage === "undefined") {
      window.digitalData.storage = {};
      return true;
    } else {
      return true;
    }
  }
  return false;
};

const setCookie = (cname, cvalue, exdays) => {
  var d = new Date();
  d.setTime(d.getTime() + exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
  document.cookie =
    cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;domain=.falabella.com";
};

/**
 *
 * Get cookie
 *
 * @param {String} cname Cookie Name
 * @returns {String} Cookie value
 */
const getCookie = (cname) => {
  var name = cname + "=";
  var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
  var ca = decodedCookie.split(";");
  for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0) == " ") {
      c = c.substring(1);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    }
  }
  return null;
};

/*************************************************************************************************************
*	Adobe Consulting Plugin: getPercentPageViewed v6.0.0
*
*	Release Date: 2021-07-26
* 
*	Arguments to Pass In:
*	@param {String} pid a variable that you want to tie the percentage of page viewed to.  This would usually be some sort of page identifier.  Defaults to the Analytics pageName OR the current URL if not set.
*	@param {Boolean} change set this equal to false if you don't want the plugin to take into consideration any changes made to the page size after its initial load.  true is the recommended/default value for this argument
*			
*	@returns {Object} 
*		An object with the following variables:
*			ppvPreviousPage = The name of the previous page viewed (Since final measurements aren't available until a NEW page loads) 
*			ppvHighestPercentViewed = The highest percent of the previous page that the visitor viewed (height-wise); in other words, what was the furthest point that the visitor scrolled down on the page
*			ppvInitialPercentViewed = The percent of the previous page that was visible when the previous page *first* loaded
*			ppvHighestPixelsSeen = The highest number of total pixels seen (height-wise) as the visitor scrolled down the previous page
*			ppvFoldsSeen = The highest number of total "page folds" seen as the visitor scrolled down the previous page (including the "top-of-page" fold)
*			ppvFoldsAvailable = The number of total "page folds" available to scroll down on the previous page 
*
*
*************************************************************************************************************/
function getPercentPageViewed(pid, change)
{
	if(pid === "-v") return {"plugin": "getPercentPageViewed", "version": "6.0.0"}
	
	window.pageName = ("undefined" !== typeof s && s.pageName) || "";

	function handlePPVevents()
	{
		//return nothing if ppvID hasn't been set yet. 
		if(!window.ppvID) return;

		var getValue = function( name ) {
			var r;
			try { r = Math.max( document.body[name], document.documentElement[name] ) } 
			catch(e) { 
				try { r = document.body[name] }
				catch(e) {
					try { r = document.documentElement[name] }
					catch(e) { r = 0 }
				}
			}
			return r;
		},
		//set documentHeight equal to the height (in pixels) of the entire web page
		documentHeight = Math.max( getValue( 'scrollHeight' ), getValue( 'offsetHeight' ), getValue( 'clientHeight' ) ),

		//set browserWindowHeight equal to the height (in pixels) of the browser window's visible portion
		browserWindowHeight = window.innerHeight || getValue( 'clientHeight' ),

		//set pixelsDown equal to the number of pixels that the visitor has scrolled down from the top of the page
		pixelsDown = window.pageYOffset || getValue( 'scrollTop' ),

		foldsSeen = Math.floor( totalPixelsSeen / browserWindowHeight ),

		//set foldsAvailable equal to the number of below-the-folds available (including the top-of-page fold)

		//4. the highest number of pixels scrolled down to on that page
		//5. the highest number of "folds" scrolled down to on the page
		//6. the highest number of folds available to scroll down to
		if(percentPixelsViewed > 0)
			cookieValue = ppvID + "," + 
			(percentPixelsViewed > highestPercentViewed ? percentPixelsViewed : highestPercentViewed) + "," +
			initialPercentViewed + "," +
			(totalPixelsSeen > highestTotalPixelsSeen ? totalPixelsSeen : highestTotalPixelsSeen) + "," +
			(foldsSeen > highestFoldsSeen ? foldsSeen : highestFoldsSeen) + "," +
			(foldsAvailable > highestFoldsAvailable ? foldsAvailable : highestFoldsAvailable);
		//write the s_ppv cookie (to be extracted on the next call)
		window.cookieWrite("s_ppv", cookieValue);
	};


	//set cookieValue equal to the s_ppv cookie
	var cookieValue = window.cookieRead("s_ppv"),

		//set cookieArray equal to the items in cookieValue
		cookieArray = cookieValue.indexOf(",") > -1 ? cookieValue.split(",") : [],

		//set pid equal to window.pageName OR the URL by default	
		pid = pid ? pid : window.digitalData.page.pageName ? window.digitalData.page.pageName : document.location.href;

	//decode the first item in cookieArray (usually pageName)
	cookieArray[0] = decodeURIComponent(cookieArray[0]);

	//set window.ppvChange to true by default (useful for measuring pages that change size)
	if(typeof change === "undefined" || change == true) window.ppvChange = true;
	else window.ppvChange = false;

	//if ppvID hasn't been set yet or if it's not equal to the pid argument's value (meaning we might have a new pageName)
	if(!window.ppvID || window.ppvID !== pid)
	{
		//set ppvID equal to the pid argument value
		window.ppvID = pid;

		//blank out the s_ppv cookie
		window.cookieWrite("s_ppv", "");

		//run the handlePPVevents plugin for the first time...
		handlePPVevents();
	}

	//if we're running this for the first time and we can addEventListener(s)
	if(window.p_fo("s_gppvLoad") && window.addEventListener)
	{
		//run handlePPVEvents on load, click, scroll, and resize events
		window.addEventListener("load", handlePPVevents, false);
		window.addEventListener("click", handlePPVevents, false);
		window.addEventListener("scroll", handlePPVevents, false);
	}

	//set the return variables
	return {
		ppvPreviousPage : cookieArray[0] ? cookieArray[0] : '',
		ppvHighestPercentViewed : cookieArray[1] ? cookieArray[1] : '',
		ppvInitialPercentViewed : cookieArray[2] ? cookieArray[2] : '',
		ppvHighestPixelsSeen : cookieArray[3] ? cookieArray[3] : '',
		ppvFoldsSeen : cookieArray[4] ? cookieArray[4] : '',
		ppvFoldsAvailable : cookieArray[5] ? cookieArray[5] : ''
	}
}

/**
 * 
 * @param {String} cname Cookie Name
 * @param {String} cvalue Cookie Value
 * @param {Number} exdays Expiration days
 */
function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
    var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;domain=.falabella.com";
}

function checkIfTesting() {
    return /hometagtest=true/i.test(document.URL) || _satellite.cookie.get('hometagtest');
}
if (checkIfTesting()) {
    if (document.querySelector('.site-wrapper')) {
        document.querySelector('.site-wrapper').style.background = "green";
    }

    document.body.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
    });

}

function addHomeTagHandlers() {
    document.addEventListener('mousedown', function(event) {
        var target = event.target;
        var elementModuleWrapper = target.closest("[data-wrapper]");
        if (elementModuleWrapper) {
            var suffix = flexibleTagging(elementModuleWrapper, target, event);
            if (suffix) {
                if (checkIfTesting()) {
                    alert(suffix);
                } else {
                    setCookie(storageImg, '', -1);
                    setCookie(storageImg, btoa(suffix.i), 1);

                    delete suffix.i;

                    setCookie(storageName, '', -1);
                    setCookie(storageName, btoa(JSON.stringify(suffix)), 1);
                }
            }
        }
    })
}

function flexibleTagging(parent, clickedElement, event) {
    var elementCTA = clickedElement.closest('[data-cta]');
    var list = elementArray('[data-cta]', parent);
    if (elementCTA && parent && list.length > 0) {
        var parentDataRef = parent.dataset.wrapper.match(/(.*)-(.*)/);
        var parentIdentifier = parentDataRef ? parentDataRef[1] : "undefined";
        var parentSectionName = parentDataRef ? parentDataRef[2] : "undefined";
        var parentPositionIndex = elementArray('[data-wrapper]').filter(function(e) {
            return e.getBoundingClientRect().width > 0 && e.getBoundingClientRect().height > 0;
        }).indexOf(parent) + 3;
        var containterCTA = elementCTA.closest('[data-cont]');
        var elementOrderNumber;
        var ctaOrderNumber;
        var nodeCheckImage;
        if (containterCTA) {
            elementOrderNumber = elementArray('[data-cont]', parent).length > 0 ? elementArray('[data-cont]', parent).indexOf(containterCTA) + 1 : 1;
            ctaOrderNumber = elementArray('[data-cta]', containterCTA).indexOf(elementCTA) + 1;
            nodeCheckImage = containterCTA;
        } else {
            elementOrderNumber = elementArray('[data-cta]', parent).indexOf(elementCTA) + 1;
            ctaOrderNumber = 1;
            nodeCheckImage = elementCTA;
        }

        var imageSource = giveImageSrc(nodeCheckImage) ? giveImageSrc(nodeCheckImage) : giveImageSrc(parent);

        return {
            d: parentIdentifier,
            dw: parentSectionName,
            pp: parentPositionIndex,
            ps: elementOrderNumber,
            i: imageSource,
            y: event.pageY
        };
    }
    return false;
}

function giveImageSrc(node) {
    var nodeImageSrc = findImage(node);
    if (nodeImageSrc) {
        return nodeImageSrc;
    }
    var nodeContainer = node.closest('[data-cont]') && node.closest('[data-cont]').parentNode || node.closest('[data-wrapper]');
    if (nodeContainer) {
        var nodeContainerImageSrc = findImage(nodeContainer);
        if (nodeContainerImageSrc) {
            return findImage(nodeContainer);
        }
    }

    return "N/A";
}

function findImage(node2) {

    var pictureQuerySelector = node2.querySelector('source') || node2.closest('source') || node2.querySelector('img') || node2.closest('img');

    if (pictureQuerySelector && pictureQuerySelector.srcset) {
        return pictureQuerySelector.srcset.replace(/\s/gi, '').split(',')[0].replace(/\.webp\d+\w+/, ".webp").replace(/\?.*/, '');
    } else if (pictureQuerySelector && pictureQuerySelector.src) {
        return pictureQuerySelector.src.replace(/\s/gi, '').split(',')[0].replace(/\.webp\d+\w+/, ".webp").replace(/\?.*/, '');
    }
}

//Utility functions
function elementArray(selector, parent) {
    return [].slice.apply((parent || document).querySelectorAll(selector));
}

/**

 * ShadowRoot

var shadowInterval = setInterval(getShadowRoots, 1500);
var shadowIntent = 0;
var shadowLimit = 5;

function getShadowRoots() {
    var shadowRoots = [];

    document.querySelectorAll('*').forEach(function(e) {
        if (e.shadowRoot) {
            shadowRoots.push({
                shadowRoot: e.shadowRoot,
                parent: e
            });
        }
    });

    if (shadowLimit < shadowIntent) {
        clearInterval(shadowInterval);
    }

    if (shadowRoots.length > 0) {

        clearInterval(shadowInterval);
        handleShadowRoots(shadowRoots);
    }

    shadowIntent++;

}

function handleShadowRoots(shadowRoots) {

    shadowRoots.forEach(function(e) {
        e.shadowRoot.addEventListener('mousedown', function(event) {

            var tagging = flexibleTagging(event.target.closest('[data-wrapper]'), event.target, event);

            setCookie(storageImg, '', -1);
            setCookie(storageImg, btoa(tagging.i), 1);

            delete tagging.i;

            setCookie(storageName, '', -1);
            setCookie(storageName, btoa(JSON.stringify(tagging)), 1);
        });
    });

}

function CyberMundosStructure(parent, clickedElement) {

        var list = elementArray('.World_world__1nii4', mundo.closest(parent.selector));

        var clickedPod = clickedElement.closest('[class*="podAnchor"]');
        var clickedPromoPod = clickedElement.closest('[class*="podPromoContainer"]');

        var clickedAllMobile = clickedElement.closest('[class*="showmoreDropdownOption"]');

            return mundoTitle + "|" + mundoOrderNumber + "|PC" + podOrder + "|" + podOrder + "|" + podDetail + "|" + podImg;

        }

            var podDetail = clickedPromoPod.href.match(/(cat\d+|staticPageId=.*|Ntt=.*|\d+)/) || undefined;

function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));

/**
 * 
 * @param {Element} element 
 */
function findAnchor(element) {
    return element.tagName != 'A' ?
        element.closest('a') ? element.closest('a') : element.querySelector('a') :
        element;
}
/**
 * 
 * @param {Element} element anchor element
 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain
 */
function isOutOfDomain(element) {
    if (element.tagName === 'A') {
        var url = element.href;
        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;
        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {
            return false;
        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {
            return true;
        }
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}
/**
 * 
 * @param {Element} element 
 * @returns {String} with Store Name
 */
function getStoreNameByElement(element) {
    if (element.tagName === 'A') {
        var url = element.href;
        //remove parameters
        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;
        return 'Store ' + (url.includes('sodimac') ? 'Sodimac' :
            url.includes('linio') ? 'Linio' :
            url.includes('tottus') ? 'Tottus' :
            url.includes('tienda') && url.includes('falabella-') ? 'Falabella' :
            'none');
    }
    return '';
}
/**
 * 
 * @param {Event} e Event
 * @param {String} level level of event (N1, N2, etc.)
 * @param {Boolean} hardAnchor boolean to hard clicked anchor
 * @param {Boolean} isStore
 * @param {String} text string to send on tag
 */
function handleEvent(e, level, hardAnchor, isStore, text) {

    var element = findAnchor(e.target);
    if (hardAnchor && !['A', 'B'].includes(e.target.tagName)) {
        if (!(text === 'UA' && element.innerText.toUpperCase() == 'MIS CMR PUNTOS' && ['P', 'DIV'].includes(e.target.tagName))) {
            return;
        }
    }

    var obj = {
        l: level,
        n: isStore ? getStoreNameByElement(element) : text && text !== 'UA' ? text : element.innerText,
        ood: isOutOfDomain(element || e)
    };

    setCookie(storageName, '', -1);
    setCookie(storageName, btoa(JSON.stringify(obj)), 1);



    if (obj.ood && _satellite) {
        _satellite.track('OOD_CALL');
    }

}

 * N1
 */

function checkDigitalData() {

 * cookie

/**
 * 
 * @param {String} cname Cookie Name
 * @param {String} cvalue Cookie Value
 * @param {Number} exdays Expiration days
 */
function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
    var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;domain=.falabella.com";
}

/**
 * 
 * @param {Element} element anchor element
 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain
 */
function isOutOfDomain(element) {
    if (element && element.tagName === 'A') {
        var url = element.href;
        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;
        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {
            return false;
        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {
            return true;
        }
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}

            secondLevelDescription = ui.secondLevelDescription(theParent());

var searchSelector = 'input[class*="SearchBar"]';
var resultAreaSelector = 'div[class*="SearchList-module_searchResults"]';
var sessionStorageName = 'typeaheadresult';

function handleEvent(el) {

    var sectionText;
    var section = el.closest('section');

    var greenResult;
    var pickedElementText = el.innerText;

    var searchTerm = document.querySelector(searchSelector);


    try {
        sectionText = section.querySelector('h6').innerText
    } catch (e) {
        sectionText = 'keyword';
        greenResult = 'en negro';
    }

    var options = section.querySelector('ul').childNodes;

    var index = getIndex(el, options);

    /**
     * When index is Not a Number, the result is inside green section
     */
    if (isNaN(index)) {
        options.forEach(function(e) {
            var ul = e.querySelector('ul');
            if (ul) {
                pickedElementText = ul.parentNode.querySelector('a').innerText;
                options = ul.childNodes;
                index = getIndex(el, options);
                greenResult = 'en verde';
            }
        });
    }
    sessionStorage.setItem(sessionStorageName,
        searchTerm.value + '|' + sectionText + '|' + pickedElementText + '|' + index + '/' + options.length + (greenResult ? '|' + greenResult : '')
    );
}

function getIndex(element, list) {
    var index;
    list.forEach(function(e, i) {
        if (e.querySelector('a').href == element.href) {
            index = i;
        }
    });
    return index + 1;
}


function execute() {
    try {
        var current = 0,
            tries = 100;
        var resultArea;

        var interval = setInterval(function() {

            resultArea = document.querySelector(resultAreaSelector);

            if (resultArea) {
                var links = resultArea.querySelectorAll('a');

                links.forEach(function(l) {
                    l.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        handleEvent(l);
                    });
                });
                clearInterval(interval);
            }


            if (tries < current) {
                clearInterval(interval);
            }

            current++;
        }, 50);
    } catch (ex) {}
}


document.addEventListener('click', function() {
    execute();
});

var inputBar = document.querySelector('#testId-SearchBar-Input');
if (inputBar) {
    inputBar.addEventListener('change', function() {
        execute();
    });
}
});</script><script>_satellite["_runScript18"](function(event, target, Promise) {
